< Text>
The prices are good, especially for this area of downtown, but you get what you pay for. The salads are basic compared to the other offerings in the WaterCourt but aren't bad and it is good to have a reasonable choice for food. Extremely limited indoor seating (2 four-tops, 1 six-top, 9 bar seats) and during the lunch hour, the employees on break take up half the seating and then leave their trash for someone (presumably another employee?) to clean up. Plenty of outdoor seating when the weather is nice. Strangely, no trash cans inside. You need to walk outside to throw away your trash...I guess that is why the employees leave their trash in the seating areas.</Text>

I usually order food to go from here (even before COVID) but when I do eat in the restaurant, I tend to order their breakfasts. I always over eat with their build-your-own breakfast, oops! Always comfort food here. I love their nachos, with everything on it. I haven't found better nachos anywhere else in town. The sandwiches are great--my go-to being the turkey club with avocado. Customer service is important and keeps people coming back, especially for me. And with good food, it really is a restaurant I love to support. I came in around noon for lunch. Prices were moderate and service was okay. Not much check back check down going on. I decided to have the ribs with fries and baked beans. Patrick Desjardins< /username>
< date>
1558547780554< /date>
<rating>2<//rating>< review>
5 stars to 2 stars after 10 months:

Original:
So far so good. Class of four children for 25$ per class of 30 minutes which seem to be in the range of you compare to water aquatic or YMCA. Nice facilities, parents are not in the class but you can pay 5$ or 7$ depending of the time to have free time in the pool (which is very limited in their schedule). Free wifi, hot water, 25$ yearly admission fee.

After 10 months:
My daughter received 2 ribbons in the first 3 months and for the next 7 nothing. My 3 years old might not be the best but she listens. However, the teachers (we tried 3 different) keep being stubborn about "gliding". My daughter got better but she wants to swim (move her feet). So, she is stuck at that level. Also, they need to go in deep water for the next level but the kid can practice deep water only 1/5 time, hence almost only one every two months. The program is NOT adapted for young kid and the teachers do not know how to change the routine to spark progress.

The staff is way too young. The supervisor decks are total douche bag. Sun glasses, big attitude, talk loudly. When I asked a question, their answer was very respectful like if the question was dumb while they had done a mistake (give twice the same level to my daughter).

The pool is DANGEROUS. I saw a boy that almost drowned because in the deep water the two teachers were not supervising the kid waiting in line. The boy went in the deep and couldn't get up. It took more than 3 seconds to the teachers to move toward the boy. I almost had the time to jump to rescue him myself... Very dangerous. Supervisor decks are not checking, they just walk around with weird attitude.

About supervisor decks, they also distract teachers with ridiculous riddle on the whiteboard and chitchat. I know, I stay on the side of the pool. Also, do NOT take the 3h30pm class because teachers are tidy up stuff 10 minutes before the end of the class to get ready for their "teachers huddle".

In short, the staff is way too young, all around 21 years old. They have "fun" there, and it looks to be a great place to "chill" as a first job, but for your own children safety and progression, I do not recommend.< /review>

< text>
This is our favorite place to eat in Stockton. We haven't been able to dine there since the pandemic turned the world upside down. But, thanks to DoorDash, we can still enjoy our favorite dishes at home.

We ordered chicken fried steaks with gravy, two side dishes each, Thai chicken salad and three different slices of pie. Garlic cheese bread came with the meal. It was all delicious!   A special mention for the salad. The lettuce  was so fresh it crunched with every bite. The steaks were perfect and there was plenty of gravy for each of us. My apple pie had a nice and flakey crust and the apple filling was so fresh one might think they were picked from a tree that morning. All in all a wonderful meal!</text>
